=== Agent 1: Blocks & Shared ===
You populate an HTML slide template with real content.

STRUCTURAL CONTRACT (read before anything else):
Every innerHTML value you return MUST mirror the TEMPLATE shown for each key:
- Keep the exact same HTML element types, class names, attributes, and nesting structure.
- Do NOT add new sections, new structural blocks, new headings, or new layout elements that are not present in the template.
- Do NOT remove or collapse existing structural elements — every element in the template must appear in your output.
- For repeating elements (table rows, list items, cards): output exactly one item per data record from SOURCE DATA. Do not cap the count to what the template shows — if the data has 9 records, output 9 rows. If the data has 2 records, output 2 rows.
- Text content must be concise — match the approximate text density of the template. Do not write paragraphs where the template shows short labels or values.
- Only data-driven text content (values, names, descriptions, metrics) and src/href values may differ from the template.
- Fixed UI labels already present in the template — such as card titles, section headings, column headers, category names, and any other structural text — MUST be copied verbatim. Never rename, rephrase, or replace them, even if a different label seems more appropriate for the data.
- Populate every data element with real values from SOURCE DATA only — do not invent or estimate.
- Never invent labels, categories, statuses, groupings, or concepts not present verbatim in the SOURCE DATA — if the data does not contain it, write n/a for that element.
Violating this breaks the slide layout irreparably.

SOURCE DATA (verbatim rows from context files — your content must be based on these):

Feature | IRM-30356 | CORE DATA HUB CAPABILITIES | AEOI, VIDA & OTHER DATA EXCHANGE | Vida PoC - Flow and example  integrations | GRC | PI30 | 2240 | p3 | To Do | *FLOW :*

{color:#505f79}1. Invoice Creation (Seller ERP/Accounting System){color}
{color:#505f79}Seller generates invoice in EN 16931 compliant format (structured XML/UBL).{color}
{color:#505f79}Integration Needed: ERP/accounting system must be able to export EN 16931 e-invoic{color}es.

_2._ *Submission / Pre-Validation (National Digital Reporting System, DRR)*
Invoice data is sent electronically to the tax authority before being delivered to the buyer.
Integration Options:  Direct API from ERP to tax authority system, or  PEPPOL Access Point that connects ERP  TO  tax authority network endpoint.
Purpose: pre-validation and acknowledgment.

*3. Validation by Tax Authority*
Tax authority checks: Invoice format (EN 16931 compliance) ,  VAT numbers and amounts ,  Business rules and optional risk checks
Outcome process: 
Accepted: unique ID and timestamp assigned
Rejected : correction requested
Integration Needed: Validation engine integrated with DRR database & ERP feedback mechanism.

{color:#505f79}4.   Invoice Delivery to Buyer
Once validated, invoice is transmitted electronically to the buyer system (ERP or e-invoicing platform).{color}
{color:#505f79}Integration Needed: PEPPOL or other secure delivery channels to buyer system.{color}

*5. Storage and EU Data Exchange*
Tax authority stores invoice data in national database.
For cross-border transactions, summary data or full invoices may be shared with EU Member States via VIES 2.0.
Integrations Needed:   
National DB from and to  VIES 2.0 interface 
Internal reporting / archival systems
Long-term *archive* of e-invoices, {*}logs{*}, and *declarations* / Security (data retention)
GDPR

*6. Reconciliation / VAT Return & Compliance*
Invoice data is used to:
Auto-populate VAT returns for the taxpayer
Pre-fill VAT declarations in OSS/IOSS or national system /Extend OSS usage   (?) 
Share summary data with EU authorities for cross-border reconciliation
Integration Needed:
DRR from/to VAT return processing system,
OSS/IOSS connectors
(Low- Optional) Payment & Banking Interfaces to verify VAT collection

*7. Monitoring and Risk Analysis*
Real-time analytics for:  Cross-checking declarations , Fraud detection ,  Audit trails and compliance reporting
Integration Needed: DRR / national DB ↔ Analytics engines / Risk management platforms

 

Other: 
Make sure the exceptions of any failures are logged 

_What is for revenue authority : a) Expand and consolidate systems like mydata (Greece) SDI (Italy) , SII (Spain) b) e-invoicing  integration, connection to VIES 2.0, e-invoicing support, c) New rules for e-Invoices, data retention, real-time reporting ,  d)  Interconnects ERP and e-Invoicing Providers with new APIs and infrastructures for real-time reporting , e) Data protection, auditing, traceability, data analytics, train personnel , specs, instructions, helpdesk._

 

– Additional
— data validation and enrichment engines for real-time submissions.
— fraud-detection analytics and risk scoring models.
— cross-matching of domestic vs. cross-border data (via VIES 2.0).
— dashboards and audit trails for inspectors and management.

Feature | IRM-30840 | CORE DATA HUB CAPABILITIES | AEOI, VIDA & OTHER DATA STORAGE | Data Storage  - National DB -Central repository for all issued and received e-invoices. | GRC | PI30 | 3733.1 | p3 | To Do | Based on [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-30356] ** 
on of the solution flow steps " *_Storage and EU Data Exchange "_* 
and thus we need to support a solution: 
 * Central repository for all issued and received e-invoices.
 * Supports tax control, audit, analytics, and EU data exchange (e.g., via {*}VIES 2.0{*}).
 * Must comply with national tax law *and* EU data protection rules (GDPR). 

 

Also to ensure: 
 * *Data integrity* (accurate, complete, auditable)
 ** *Immutable (WORM) storage:* prevent tampering or deletion.
 ** *Retention automation:* apply expiry dates and legal-hold exceptions.
 ** *Allow Integrity checks:* hash verification and periodic audits.

 * *Scalability & performance* (handles national volume)
 * *Interoperability* (VIES 2.0, EU standards)
 * *Security & privacy compliance* (GDPR + national law)
 * *Governance & traceability* (audit-ready at all times)

 
----
+*Solution Considerations*+ 
 * *Core* 
 ** *Structured DB + payload store:* relational DB (e.g., PostgreSQL) for key fields; object/WORM storage for full files.
{*}Scaling{*}
*Checksum*
*Storage & indexing:* fast access to invoice metadata and totals; keep original payloads for audit.{*}{{*}}
 ** *Schema*
*Ingestion & validation:* accept e-invoices in various formats (UBL, CEN, XML); check syntax and business rules
{*}Canonical data model:{*} normalize invoices into a consistent schema for processing and reporting.

 * *Integrations*
 ** *Exchange integration:* interface with VIES 2.0 and other EU Member States (summary or full invoices).
{*}VIES 2.0 adapter:{*} validate VAT IDs, send/receive cross-border summaries or full invoices.
 ** *Internal systems:* link to taxpayer master, audit, analytics, and archival modules.
 ** *Reporting/export:* feed BI dashboards and legal reports.

 *  *Auditing & Reporting*
 ** *Search & reporting:* support compliance queries, risk analysis, and statistical reporting.
 ** *Audit & traceability:* log every event—submission, modification, access, and exchange.

 

--------------------------------------------

Notes - 
 * Monitoring, alerting, and reconciliation for VIES exchanges.

 * Backup, disaster recovery, and business-continuity planning.

 * Role segregation: operations / auditors / developers.

 * Periodic reviews of exemption and retention configurations.

Feature | IRM-29513 | REFERENCE IMPLEMENTATIONS | APPLICATION PROCESSES | Support four-eye principle in Solon Tax - Approval Workflow | GRC | PI29 | 392 | p3 | Waiting Analysis Approval | As an IRM Admin, I should be able to configure workflows, that enforce four-eyes approval within business processes, ensuring that one user initiates an action and a different user validates and approves it before completion.

*Introduction* 

This feature is a result of PSD-12702 for UBM project, however it is anticipated that all implementations may use this functionality to cover different business cases. As it is described in the related PSD: 

At present, SOLON does not support double attestation (four eye principle) out of the box in human case management, which conflicts with the following requirement specified in SKV's contract (applicable to UBM as well):

 
|​3.2.2.2.1.16|​Functional|​Case Management|​In the software, it shall be possible to configure the actions that require verification (double attestation) by two different case workers during manual handling, including at least:
 - Manual registration of debiting/crediting
 - Manual modification of a transaction on a tax account
 - Manual administration of Swedish and foreign disbursement accounts
 - Manual registration and modification of a disbursement block​|​LKVFM-2.9.306|

 

UBM need the possibility to employ double attestation on human tasks, such that a change affected by the completion of the case is verified by at least 2 distinct case workers. This is for example needed for imposing sanctions on either individual people, credit institutions, or countries, where one case worker would create the case, and another one would validate the right target is being sanctioned, approve the case, turn it back to the initiator, who could then complete the task and thereby enforce the sanction. A rejection should naturally not enforce anything, but require a change in the human task from the initiator, or closing of the case altogether. 

Dependent user stories for sanctions are attached as a PNG. They are not yet created as User Stories in toolkit. Furthermore manual registration of payment methods (e.g. for international bank accounts) require double attestation. It is expected that more functional cases that require double attestation will appear. As such, a generic approach to employing double attestation on a human task flow is needed.

A workaround is being worked on that could support double attestation, but is a process that requires a lot of manual setup (see attachment). If SOLON had the capability of staging a change for entities in a human task (without persisting it), waiting for either approval or rejection, the requirements for double attestation would be a simpler task to support. 

*Functional Requirements*

> An admin must be able to create, edit, and delete workflow templates for different business processes

> An admin must be able to configure the states (e.g., {_}Pending → Submitted → Approved → Completed{_}) and transitions between them. 

> An admin must be able to define one or more approval steps within a workflow. 

> An admin must be able to assign which roles (e.g., Maker, Checker) can perform each workflow step. 

> An admin must be able to enforce that the same user cannot perform both maker and checker roles in the same workflow instance. 

> An admin must be able to define rules for assigning checkers (e.g., based on transaction type, workers profile, business unit, availability).

> An admin must be able to configure whether one or multiple checkers are required before an item moves forward. 

> An admin must be able to set conditions (e.g., value thresholds, registration characteristics) that trigger additional approval steps. 

> An admin must be able to configure escalation paths if approvals are delayed beyond a defined time. 

> An admin must be able to configure which users(roles) receive notifications when an action is required.

> An admin must be able to set reminder frequencies and escalation notifications. 

> An admin must be able to configure who can view pending, approved, or rejected workflow items. 

> An admin must be able to monitor the status of workflow instances (pending, approved, rejected, completed).

> An admin must be able to ensure all workflow actions are logged with user ID, timestamp, and action type. 

> An admin must be able to generate reports on workflow performance (e.g., approval times, bottlenecks, compliance with four-eyes). 

> An admin must be able to define workflow steps once and reuse them across different business processes. 

> An admin must be able to configure workflows without coding, using parameters (roles, thresholds, states). 

> An admin _must be able to maintain multiple versions of a workflow template and activate/deactivate them as needed._

Feature | IRM-30636 | OTHER ACTIVITIES | APPSEC TEAM | SOLONTAX Supply Chain Security Enablement | Other | PI30 | 2240 | p3 | To Do | This enabler targets the end-to-end improvement of software supply chain security across development operations by adopting related best practices (CIS benchmark, NIST SSDF, SLSA, OWASP SCVS).{*}Scope includes:{*}

*1. Benchmark Assessment*
 * Conduct an initial assessment of existing software supply chain processes and tools against the CIS benchmark control families (Governance, Source Code, Build, Dependencies, Deployment, Monitoring).
 * Identify compliance gaps and improvement areas.

*2. Governance & Policy Definition*
 * Update a Supply Chain Security practices in the security plan.
 * Establish ownership, maintenance procedures, and periodic review cycles.

*3. Source Code & Dependency Security*
 * Enforce secure repository configurations (signed commits, branch protection, access control).
 * Integrate Software Composition Analysis (SCA) and open-source dependency validation.
 * Generate and maintain Software Bill of Materials (SBOMs) for all products.

*4. Build & CI/CD Pipeline Hardening*
 * Review and harden CI/CD configurations per CIS benchmark controls:
 ** Credential and secret management
 ** Build agent isolation
 ** Artifact integrity validation
 ** Controlled use of third-party build steps/plugins
 ** Enable artifact signing and reproducible builds.

*5. Artifact & Deployment Integrity*
 * Enforce signed artifacts and signature verification during deployments.
 * Apply access and retention controls for artifact repositories.

*6. Monitoring, Compliance & Continuous Improvement*
 * Automate CIS benchmark validation where possible.
 * Conduct regular re-assessments and track remediation progress.
 * Provide compliance dashboards and evidence for audits.
Feature | IRM-30636 | OTHER ACTIVITIES | APPSEC TEAM | SOLONTAX Supply Chain Security Enablement | Other | PI29 | 240 | p3 | To Do | This enabler targets the end-to-end improvement of software supply chain security across development operations by adopting related best practices (CIS benchmark, NIST SSDF, SLSA, OWASP SCVS).{*}Scope includes:{*}

*1. Benchmark Assessment*

 * Identify compliance gaps and improvement areas.

 ** Credential and secret management
 ** Build agent isolation
 ** Artifact integrity validation
 ** Controlled use of third-party build steps/plugins
 ** Enable artifact signing and reproducible builds.

*5. Artifact & Deployment Integrity*
 * Enforce signed artifacts and signature verification during deployments.
 * Apply access and retention controls for artifact repositories.

*6. Monitoring, Compliance & Continuous Improvement*
 * Automate CIS benchmark validation where possible.
 * Conduct regular re-assessments and track remediation progress.
 * Provide compliance dashboards and evidence for audits.

Feature | IRM-37825 | CORE REVENUE MANAGEMENT CAPABILITIES | BILLING, ASSESSMENTS AND INSTALLMENTS | Transfer Amount - Enhancement on configuration of Bill segment types | GRC | PI28 | 298.9 | p1 | In Design | As an admin, I need to configure the bill segment types generated by the Transfer Amount process so they align with existing, predefined bill segment configurations used in other relevant procedures (e.g., for the same revenue types and bill segment categories).

In the as-is, one Bill segment type is defined and be used for source and target bill segments.

 

*Functional Requirements*

 

*A) New Bill Segment Type field, next to existing:* 
 * Alternative Target Bill segment type 
Lookup bill segment type and filters may be used to locate proper type.
 * Optional field
 * Add Tooltip: This value applies to the target bill segment if filled. If no filled the default bill segment type will be applied to target bill segment as in source bill segment. 
 * Add it in search filters.

*B) Existing Bill Segment Type field:*
 * New label : Default Bill segment type
 * Be able to search by  using fields to locate proper type.
 * Add Tooltip: This value applies to the source bill segment and will also be applied to the target bill segment unless a different bill segment type is explicitly selected.

Consideration : Bill type should support both bill segment types. 

 

*C) Mechanism:*
 * Default bill segment type is mandatory. 
 * Default Bill segment type will be used for source bill segment.
 * Alternative Target Bill segment type  will be used for target bill segment.
 * If Alternative Target Bill segment type id not filled, then Default Bill segment type will be used for target bill segment.

 

*Documentation*
Document all the above adjustments.

Performance , Security, Accessibility, Usability  
It is expected that all DODs are fulfilled.
Feature | IRM-19514 | CORE REVENUE MANAGEMENT CAPABILITIES | BILLING, ASSESSMENTS AND INSTALLMENTS | Add and Maintain Ad-hoc Obligations – Pay Instalment Actions and Categories | GRC | PI28 | 560 | p1 | HLD | For Ad-hoc obligations : 
As a revenue official, I want to see that a party in a specific role was, is or is going to be obliged to pay an assessment in instalments, so that I can check whether this party in a specific role is meeting the obligation to pay these instalments on time and in full and can take measures if this is not the case. i.e, I need to be able to add several payment action under an ad-hoc obligations to represent Installments similarly to what is happening in the Periodic Obligations.  
This can be used for Inheritance tax, legacy data migration processes, other cases like Guarantees. 

The goal is to be able to add more than payment obligation actions per obligation for ad-hoc obligations, similarly to what happens with periodic obligations. 

Relevant : [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-11522] , [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-10419] 

*Functional Requirements*

*Basics*
 * User and admin can create multiple payment obligation actions under an ad-hoc obligation (revenue type category = Ad-hoc)  as installments or even as onceoff , following the structure of the non ad-hoc obligations with installments. 
 ** User can add a Filing and more that one Payment Actions in ad-hoc Obligation (flagged as Installments or once off) 
 ** User can define the Category as is in periodic ones : Preliminary, Original
 ** User can defile the subtype of the Obligation action (now available in c_revenue_calendar_period_action for periodic only). Values: Once-Off, Installment, Amendment. 
Default value : Once-Off, Optional for ad-hocs (no need to create breaking change) 
If values from calendar, then defined by system, if ad-hoc admin may define. 
 ** User can define the due date (as happens now)
 ** Status is managed by the system (as happens now). 
 ** One Filing OA  per category (preliminary or Original) is only permitted. 
 ** More than one are permitted for Payment OAs 
 ** Details of category and subtype are visible in UI.
 * User may define in a new field Payment reference" text 500 characters , the payment reference
 ** User may search by this  new field Payment reference  and see this in UI. 
 * User can see the list of pay instalment actions that a party in a specific role -  was, is or is going to be  - obliged to perform for a specific revenue type for a specific revenue period or once-off. User can see information that identifies a pay instalment action and its status to the user, such as action category (e.g. preliminary or original), action type, action reference number, action due date, amount and action status (e.g. active or closed).
 * User can create manually the payment obligation actions (as happens now).
 * User can sort the list.
 * User can open a pay instalment action to see more details and update if needed. 

 

-*Advanced:*- 

-*Additional functionality:*- 
-To be able for the user to create several installments, a set of predefined rules may be ready in a way that  :- 
-User will add some parameters such as already logged start date, due date , will add some additional such as : number of installments,  duration between installments, type of action (payment) to be created and margin to grace date. Will click a button and installments will be created.  Then user will be able to update the entries.- 
 * -Admin can define the rule in the revenue type on how  to create the installments for ad-hoc revenue types (suggestion : Dynamic Rules)- 
 ** -Rules will be able via parameters added by user to generate payment actions under an ad-hoc obligation.-  
 ** -Rule will calculate a) the ad-hoc installments / payment actions :  according set by user start date, duration between installments , number of installments , margin of grace date, category . b) Filing actions according Start date , due date of the obligation, margin of Grace date , category-

-+Consideration+-
-User should be able to define the rule to create the installments (e.g.  Dynamic Rules or batches)- 
-Rules should be able via parameters added by user to generate payment actions under an ad-hoc obligation.-  
-Rule may calculate a) the ad-hoc installments / payment actions :  according set by user start date, duration between installments , number of installments , margin of grace date, category . b) Filing actions according Start date , due date of the obligation, margin of Grace date , category-

 

*Documentation*
Document all the above adjustments. 

 

*Non functional requirements*
It is expected that the NFRs are considered and examined: Performance , Security, Accessibility, Usability 

DODs should be fulfilled.

Feature | IRM-12465 | CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | CASE MANAGEMENT | Define and Maintain Case Type - Case Worker Profiles - Use Availability - Admin | GRC | PI29 | 392 | p3 | Waiting Analysis Approval | As an admin, I want to use the case worker’s availability as a criterion in a case worker’s profile. So that only case workers that have a certain availability can be assigned to cases for which this case worker’s profile is applicable.

*Introduction*

This feature extends IRM-702 in which requirements have been documented to define what case worker’s profiles are required to perform a certain type of case.

*Functional Requirements*
 * Admin can use the following matching criteria when defining profiles for the most suitable case workers for a specific type of case:
 ** Average Allocation: can be calculated by dividing the sum of the allocated effort of a worker within a given period (from the start date up until the end date of a case) by the sum of the available man-hours in that same period based on the resource calendars that are effective for the case worker in that period. Admin can for example define that the average allocation should be equal to or less than 0.8.
 ** Available man-hours: can be calculated by subtracting the sum of the allocated effort of a case worker within a given period (from the start date up until the end date of a case) from the sum of the available man-hours in that same period based on the resource calendars that are effective for the case worker in that period. Admin can for example define that a worker should at least have 8 hours unallocated man-hours within a period.
Feature | IRM-12465 | CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | CASE MANAGEMENT | Define and Maintain Case Type - Case Worker Profiles - Use Availability - Admin | GRC | PI28 | 42 | p3 | Waiting Analysis Approval | As an admin, I want to use the case worker’s availability as a criterion in a case worker’s profile. So that only case workers that have a certain availability can be assigned to cases for which this case worker’s profile is applicable.

*Introduction*

This feature extends IRM-702 in which requirements have been documented to define what case worker’s profiles are required to perform a certain type of case.

*Functional Requirements*
 * Admin can use the following matching criteria when defining profiles for the most suitable case workers for a specific type of case:
 ** Average Allocation: can be calculated by dividing the sum of the allocated effort of a worker within a given period (from the start date up until the end date of a case) by the sum of the available man-hours in that same period based on the resource calendars that are effective for the case worker in that period. Admin can for example define that the average allocation should be equal to or less than 0.8.
 ** Available man-hours: can be calculated by subtracting the sum of the allocated effort of a case worker within a given period (from the start date up until the end date of a case) from the sum of the available man-hours in that same period based on the resource calendars that are effective for the case worker in that period. Admin can for example define that a worker should at least have 8 hours unallocated man-hours within a period.
Feature | IRM-12464 | CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | CASE MANAGEMENT | Add and Maintain Case - Assign and Unassign Case Workers - Effort - User | GRC | PI29 | 392 | p3 | Waiting Analysis Approval | As a revenue official, I want to assign case workers (user) that have a required profile (e.g. skills, experience and part of a certain organizational unit) to a case while also considering the availability of the suitable candidates, so that a capable worker (user) with sufficient availability can work on and complete the case. Also, I want to see how much effort is involved for each assigned case worker and for the case in total.

*Introduction*

This feature extends IRM-680 in which requirements have been documented to assign and unassign a worker to/from a case. IRM-680 includes a requirement that the user can specify the expected allocation of a case worker for a case.

This feature is related to IRM-12459 in which requirements have been documented to assign and unassign one or more resource calendars to a worker.

*Functional Requirements*
 * Eligible Workers
 ** User can see the average allocation from the case start date up until the case end date for each case worker that meets any of the worker’s profiles for the case. Average allocation can be calculated by dividing the sum of the allocated effort of a case worker from the start date up until the end date of a case by the sum of the available man-hours in that same period based on the resource calendars that are effective for the case worker in that period
 ** User can see the availability in man-hours from the case start date up until the case end date for each case worker that meets any of the case worker’s profiles for the case. Available man-hours can be calculated by subtracting the sum of the allocated effort for a case worker from the start date up until the end date of a case from the sum of the available man-hours in that same period based on the resource calendars that are effective for the case worker in that period.
 * Worker’s Assignment
 ** User can see what effort has been calculated based on the provided expected allocation for the case worker’s assignment and the resource calendar(s) that are effective for this worker from the case start date up until the case end date. Effort can only be calculated if (1) a start date and end date have been defined for the related case, and (2) an expected allocation has been provided. Period(s) within the start and end date of the case for which no effective resource calendar has been defined for the case worker are considered non-working periods. Assumption is that the effort will be recalculated if (1) the case start or end date are updated, (2) the expected allocation for that case worker for that case is updated, and/or (3) a resource calendar of an assigned case worker that falls within the period in which the case has been scheduled, is updated.
 * User can see the total calculated effort for the case. Total effort is equal to the sum of the effort that was calculated for each case worker that was assigned to the case.

Feature | IRM-542 | REFERENCE IMPLEMENTATIONS | CIT | CIT - Submit a CIT Return on ICARUS Self Service | Other | PI30 | 130.9 | p3 | Under Analysis | As an ICARUS Self Service user, I want to submit a CIT Return form that captures all necessary Information needed to create a tax assessment for CIT.

*Prerequisites*
 An entity should be:
 1. Registered in IRM System, thus have a TIN
 2. Registered for CIT in IRM
 prior to submit a CIT return form.

The following *actions* should be available in ICARUS Self Service: 
 1. Open a CIT Return form, from the list of existing filing obligations.
 2. Create a CIT Return form and save it as a draft. User should be able to open the draft at a later point and proceed with editing.
 3. Print a CIT Return form in a PDF format should be available.
 4. Submit a CIT Return form to the back-end system.

5. Taxpayer should be able to see the submission date ie the date the form was submitted to the revenue authority. 

6. Taxpayer should be able to see a unique form reference number.

 

The following *validations* on the CIT Return form should be available in ICARUS Self Service. Note that these are only sample validation rules since these may differentiate per country:
 # In Section "Filing Period Details" Fields "Filing Period Start and End Dates" create a validation for filing period based on the filing frequency defined to verify the period selected is complaint. Ex. If filing frequency is annual then 12 month period should be selected.
 # In Section "Filing Period Details" Field "If you do not have to complete ... please tick this box" create a validation when this field is selected then remaining input amount sections to calculate CIT should not be available to edit. Tax amount for this period should be set to zero. 
 # In Section "Net Income" only fields "Returns and Allowances, Cost of Goods Sold, Depreciation and Amortization" should be allowed to accept negative values (Zero value should be allowed). 
 # In Section "Final Tax Assessment"when field "Other Adjustments" has a value different than zero then Attachment Category "Miscellaneous related attachments" should be required prior submitting the form.

Using functionality as defined by the solution of [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-435]    **    ,  we may define the Document using a specific format.

 * -Example / Base rule to format the Reference ID  :  **-

 -c) Related party role primary Identifier-
 -d)- {-}Seperator "{-}"-
  -e)  YYYTMMDDHH (Year 4 digits + Month 3 digits+ Day 2 digits + HH+MM+SS)-
  {-}d)  Seperator "{-}"- 
  -e) String that will be "IN" for Inbound documents,  "OUT" for Outbound documents, "SYS" for System generated documents-

Document all the above adjustments.

-More details on Legal requirements for Documents :- 
 -LT:- 
|-Every document, whether incoming or system-generated (e.g. forms, letters), must receive a unique registration number.-
-Forms are documents, so forms submitted by users must also have metadata as below:.-|
||-Field-||-Description-||
|-*Document Name*-|-Human-readable title-|
|-*Creator / Author*-|-User or system module creating the document-|
|-*Sender / Receiver*-| * -For sent docs: add recipient.-
 * -For received docs: record sender, their reg. number, original date/title.-|
|-*Date*-|-Created and registered timestamps, YYYY-MM-DD-|
|-*Registration Number*-|-MAP automatically assigns a unique document registration number with a prefix and yearly resetting counter (e.g., 2025-IN-0001, 2025-OUT-0002).-|
|-*Original Document Ref.*-|-Links to the original document (e.g. response to request)-|

-Depending on the document type{*},{*} additional metadata fields may be required (e.g., contact email, case ID, type of correspondence).|-
Feature | IRM-790 | CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | CONTACT MANAGEMENT | Send Outbound Message Automatically to Multiple Recipients - Admin | GRC | PI29 | 358.4 | p3 | Waiting Analysis Approval | As an admin, I want to automatically send a copy of a specific outbound message (e.g. letter, email or text message) to different types of recipients (e.g. taxpayer and tax agent), so that the information in the outbound message can be exchanged with all relevant parties.

*Introduction*

This feature extends IRM-786 and IRM-789 where requirements have been documented to send an outbound letter and outbound email / text messages automatically to a single party.

*Functional Requirements*

Admin can enter literal values and/or reference values that will be known at run-time for input parameters that admin has defined for this type of contact and that can be used to automatically select the type of recipients that need to be considered for this type of outbound message, and automatically select a recipient for each type of recipient (based on rules defined by admin). These values can be defined on a 'establish and/or record contact' task within a specific type of business process (see IRM-785).

When executing the 'establish and/or record contact' task on an instance of this type of business process, the system will automatically generate all outbound messages, store these messages, finalize the messages, select a communication channel for each recipient and send the finalized outbound messages via the selected communication channels (e.g. print letter or send email).

Feature | IRM-775 | CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | CONTACT MANAGEMENT | Define and Maintain Contact Types - Select Recipients - Admin | GRC | PI29 | 392 | p3 | Waiting Analysis Approval | As an admin, I want to define and maintain rules to determine what recipient(s) need to receive a copy of a certain type of outbound message (e.g. certain type of letter, email or SMS), so that duplicate messages can be send to all parties that need to be informed.

*Introduction*

This feature extends IRM-772 in which requirements have been documented to define and maintain different types of contacts.

Recipients will receive the same information or almost the same information. For example, one letter could contain text to explain that this letter is a copy of the letter that has been sent to the taxpayer representative.
Relevant to https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-774 

*Functional Requirements*
 * Admin can define rules to determine what types of recipients must receive a copy of a specific type of outbound message under certain circumstances. For example, if a certain type of letter is sent to the recipient type 'taxpayer' then a copy of this letter may have to be sent to the recipient type 'tax agent' and/or recipient type 'spouse'.
 * Admin can define rules to determine the recipient for each type of recipient that will receive a copy of the message. For example, find the 'tax agent' that is representing a 'taxpayer' for a specific type of tax. Input parameters defined on the contact type can be used to select the recipients. Values for these input parameters can be provided at design time (literal values) or can be provided at run-time.

Feature | IRM-766 | CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | CONTACT MANAGEMENT | Send Outbound Message Manually to Multiple Recipients - User | GRC | PI29 | 739.2 | p1 | Waiting Analysis Approval | As a revenue official, I want to send a copy/version of a specific outbound message (e.g. letter, email or text message) to different types of recipients (e.g. taxpayer and tax agent), so that the information in the outbound message can be exchanged with all relevant parties.

*Introduction*

This feature extends IRM-762 and IRM-765 where requirements have been documented to send an outbound letter and outbound email / text message manually to a single party.
Admin feature to support this is the IRM-26951 

*Functional Requirements*
 * *Select recipients*
 ** User can select to send a contact to multiple recipients instead of one party role if contact type allows this usage. Option appears to the user to load a list. 
 *** Optionally select to upload a file with party role IDs.  The party roles appears in a list. 
 *** Optionally may add recipients manually selecting them and adding in the list. 
 *** Optionally may select one recipient from the list and click to remove it.
 *** The contact is send using one record of contact as per the channel selected. -The preferred contact is selected if applicable.-
-(Note: it is better to use systems contact details to avoid improper usage of persons emails)-  
 ** -User will create the parent contact as per contact type.-
 *** -It is expected system , per recipient to generate/send a new contact  - as a child contact to parent contact created.-  
 *** -The child contacts should be visible under the parent contact-
 ** User will select one channel. 
 * *Generation and results*
 ** User can generate the outbound messages/emails for the recipients selected.
 ** Different types of recipients may receive different outbound message content. (Based on [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-774] ) Admin need to define the contact template per recipient.  
Examples: 
One outbound message could contain text to explain that this outbound message is a copy of the outbound message that has been sent to another type of recipient.
Address requested in contact template as well as balance is adjusted as per party selected. 
Generation requirements as documented in IRM-762 and IRM-765 also apply when sending outbound messages to multiple recipients. (to be moved to a new feature).
 ** User can regenerate the outbound messages. Regeneration requirements as documented in IRM-762 and IRM-765 also apply when sending outbound messages to multiple recipients.
 ** User can finalize the generated outbound messages.
 ** User can send the finalized outbound messages via the selected communication channel. Send requirements as documented in IRM-762 and IRM-765 also apply when sending outbound messages to multiple recipients.
 ** User can store the outbound messages. Storage requirements as documented in IRM-762 and IRM-765 also apply when sending outbound messages to multiple recipients.
 ** User can see the results of the emailing/sms if integration allows so (as per  IRM-27816 ) 
 ** Solution should be applicable to [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-28177] 
 * *Exceptions*
 ** Errors/exceptions appears if one of the recipients have incorrect/missing contact details for the selected channel and none of the batch  is sent. 
"Mass contact generation failed" 
"Mass contact send failed" 
Note: it is expected is user does not have access as per row level security to the party role, cannot select party role in the list described above.
 ** Errors/exceptions appears if any of the contacts cannot generate proper content - parameters are missing. 
 * *History*
 ** All Actions and list of sent contacts should be logged in audit trail
 * *Admin leftovers*
 ** Make visible admin items implemented in [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-26951]

Address requested in contact template as well as balance is adjusted as per party selected. 
Generation requirements as documented in IRM-762 and IRM-765 also apply when sending outbound messages to multiple recipients. (to be moved to a new feature).
 ** User can regenerate the outbound messages. Regeneration requirements as documented in IRM-762 and IRM-765 also apply when sending outbound messages to multiple recipients.
 ** User can finalize the generated outbound messages.
 ** User can send the finalized outbound messages via the selected communication channel. Send requirements as documented in IRM-762 and IRM-765 also apply when sending outbound messages to multiple recipients.
 ** User can store the outbound messages. Storage requirements as documented in IRM-762 and IRM-765 also apply when sending outbound messages to multiple recipients.
 ** User can see the results of the emailing/sms if integration allows so (as per  IRM-27816 ) 
 ** Solution should be applicable to [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-28177] 
 * *Exceptions*
 ** Errors/exceptions appears if one of the recipients have incorrect/missing contact details for the selected channel and none of the batch  is sent. 
"Mass contact generation failed" 
"Mass contact send failed" 
Note: it is expected is user does not have access as per row level security to the party role, cannot select party role in the list described above.
 ** Errors/exceptions appears if any of the contacts cannot generate proper content - parameters are missing. 
 * *History*
 ** All Actions and list of sent contacts should be logged in audit trail
 * *Admin leftovers*
 ** Make visible admin items implemented in [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-26951]

Feature | IRM-28521 | CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | DOCUMENT MANAGEMENT INTEGRATION | Generic component - Support for Embedded 3rd-Party Digital Signature and Document Preview Components in RM pages | Other | PI30 | 104.30000000000001 | p1 | Closed | As an delivery team and admin I need the ability to integrate 3rd-party components such as digital signature dialogs and embedded document/PDF previewers into the Solon UI, so that we can support customer-specific implementations.
As a revenue authority user, I want to preview forms and assist taxpayers in digitally signing documents directly within the Registration Module (RM), in order to comply with national requirements and improve support service at physical desks.

On these Solon will not provide any out of the self integration with these tools but will provide a widget to enable partners on that. 

*Introduction*

According to the Lithuanian law, when signing documents electronically, the user should be able to preview the document in the Web page. Furthermore, the customers want to be able to preview signed or unsigned documents within the web app.
Moreover, there are user flows provided by the client, where users need to preview PDF documents directly within the application. However, the current UI/JSON schema system does not support rendering or embedding PDF viewers, making it impossible to include this functionality through the schema.

Currently, Solon's UI metadata schema (UI/JSON) does not support rendering embedded components like PDF viewers or signature popups. As a result, these features cannot be implemented declaratively through configuration alone. Similar components will be used in ISS by LT delivery teams  (using external portal platform). 
Relevant: 
[https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/PSD-11428]
[https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/PSD-12028] 

Solon {*}will not deliver native integrations with specific 3rd-party signature providers or preview tools{*}. However, to support flexibility and enable integration at project level, Solon will provide a generic UI extension mechanism (widget) that can be configured to load and render such external components.

+Considerations+ 
 * _This widget/tag will allow embedding or linking to external components,  such as:_
 ** _PDF  document viewers (e.g. in form page preview form and attachments in a relevant preview mode)_
 *** _External digital signature modules._
_WHAT IS/could be  INCLUDED IN THE iframe and the support of all its usages is Out of scope_ 
_In scope: Be able to add iframes in modals and pages._ 
 ** _The new tag if used in an appropriate widget that is expected to be implemented by delivery , it will be able to support_ 
 *** _rendering the embedded content inline_ 
 *** _or  opening it as a dialog/popup/modal. (such as receiving input request from digital signature app)_
 *** _being triggerable by actions of user (e.g. sign button)_
 *** _pass parameters  via urls or post messages_ 
 *** _return control to Solon tax ui on success of the process (e.g. sign properly) ._ 

 

*Functional requirements*
 * A new *custom widget framework  (i.e.*  *widget-based framework* *using* *secure iframe embedding)* will be introduced in the UI schema system.
 ** Product based on type of widget  (pdf viewer, digital signature)  the proper sandbox attributes should be used
(iframes preferably should have the {{sandbox}} attribute to restrict the content of the embedded page. Any features that are needed (execute scripts, submit forms, etc.) can be explicitly enabled per case when needed).
 ** Closing window callbacks may be functional. 
 ** Be agnostic to signature providers.
 ** Be reusable / configurable 

Out of scope : 
Ui interaction/ post messages 
Custom error messages 

 

*Assumption* :
Integration is {*}properly implemented{*}.
The delivery teams must ensure that the embedded solutions conform to {*}data protection{*}, {*}security policies{*}, and *access control rules* already applied in Solon.

 

*Documentation*

Document all the above adjustments and any suggestion on good usage of the iframe while posting messages. 

 

*Non functional requirements*

Performance and Security DODs should be fulfilled.

!image-2025-07-28-21-14-34-600.png|width=1146,height=625!

 

 
----
Flow :

*E-Signature Workflow Overview*
 # *User Initiates Signing* (frontend)

The user clicks the *"Sign"* button.
 # *Signing Initialization Request* (backend)

A request is sent to the {*}electronic signature service{*}, which:
 * Uploads the files to the {*}signature provider{*}.
 * Initializes the signing process with a specified returnUrl, used to redirect the user back to our system after signing.
 * Returns an {*}external signing UID{*}.

 # *Popup with Embedded Signing UI* (frontend)

A popup window is opened containing an iframe.
The iframe loads the signing page using the URL that includes the *external signing UID* as a query parameter.

*_[DASKALAKIS Ioannis] Please provide, if possible, some more details on the authentication and authorization scheme that may need to be followed to facilitate loading service’s provider URL for the given UID with  the User’s  browser session._*

*_No authentication needs to be done from the browser. Only the backend IP needs to be whitelisted on the service provider and our service accepting the callback needs to be exposed and reachable by the service provider. We have started a discussion about this on another channel, still waiting for a response._*
 # *User Signs Documents* (frontend)

The user completes the signing process within the loaded iframe page.
 # *Callback and Document Handling* (backend)

Our service receives a *callback* from the signature provider when the document status changes (e.g., signing completed).
At this point, we:
 * {*}Download{*}the signed version of the document from the provider.
 * {*}Validate{*}the signed document.
 * {*}Upload{*}it via the document-management

*_[DASKALAKIS Ioannis] This, along with #3, suggests that any document exchange between our system and the signature provider will only take place via service API calls with an adapter implemented in the scope of the project. Please confirm._*

*_Yes, that is correct._*
 # *User Redirection and UI Update* (frontend)

After signing, the user sees a *success message* on the provider's page and is *redirected to the* {*}returnUrl{*}.
If we are able to detect this redirect within the popup, we can:
 * Automatically {*}close the popup{*}.
 * {*}Load the signed document{*}and its metadata in our system for the user to review.

*_[DASKALAKIS Ioannis] Is this required to be a document preview functionality, or it is a direct document download?_*

*_Preview is required according to project requirements._*

Feature | IRM-36668 | CORE SUPPORTING CAPABILITIES | DOCUMENT MANAGEMENT INTEGRATION | Digital Signatures - System digital signing of PDF documents generated by bpmn process | GRC | PI28 | 1344 | p1 | In Design | As a revenue authority user, when the system generates a document (e.g., operational reports, letters, certificates) and the business process instructs so, I want the document to be digitally signed by the system, with all required visual elements rendered in the PDF, so that I can securely distribute officially signed documents to taxpayers and stakeholders.

This capability must be reusable, configurable, auditable, and resilient to failures.

*Background :*
In the current (as-is) systems:
Documents are generated via operational reports 
Documents may be instructed to be generated via BPMN flows.
Documents may be sent to contacts and/or stored as attachments. 
Attachments can be linked to a Document Management System (DMS) via integration.

*Assumptions :* 
*a)* Revenue authority will supplied by an External provider the digital stamp (ψηφιακή σφραγίδα) in ΡΕΜ or PKC#7 files
Then the configurations for digital signs and certificate will be used for documents signature. 
./pdf_sign_pem_multicert <input_pdf> <output_pdf> <cert.pem> <key.pem>

for our tests we need to use one from CA authority 
*b)* Any additional elements (document IDs, DMS URLs, QR codes) must be printed on the document via project-specific implementation.
{*}c){*}Attachments are integrated with a DMS per customer configuration and responsibility.
*d)* One reference configuration for one digital signature will be only will be available for testing purposes (as demo). If projects needs several signatures, they may be able to configure them in the system.  

*Out of Scope* (for now)
End-user personal digital signatures
Non-PDF document formats
Additional IDs or other document additional elements other than digital signature. (document ID, qr code)

 

 

*Functional Requirements*

*Digital Signature service* 
 * Documents can be digitally signed when instructed by a step in a BPMN flow.
 * The system must expose an API or internal service or other method  for digital signing that can be called by bpmn processes.
 * The signing service must support the signature based on customers configurations and certificate.
 * Admin may configure several signatures.  (May be able to use more than one configurations and certificate / different signatures and bpmn process should decide on which configurations and certificate to be used, but will not be any defaults available in the product).  
 * Keep Audit log for the documents' updates.

*PDF* 
 * The digital signature must be embedded in the PDF according to industry standards (e.g., PAdES).
 * The PDF must remain verifiable by standard PDF readers.

*Storage & Metadata*
 * Signed documents must be stored as attachments  (expected as per relevant integration to be synchronized with the DMS).

 * Document generated is expected to be displayed with  the relevant signature stamp and document ID  (by a reserve id method optionally to be used  in the upload  and that may be used if  needed by configurators) 

*Visual Elements on Document*
Signed documents must display a visible digital signature stamp.

*Unhappy path :*
 * Errors must be logged and be visible.   
 ** Exceptions should be thrown if document generation or digital signature process not completed successfully. 
examples: Document generation fails, Template not found, Missing parameters, Digital signing fails, Timeouts

 

*Reference implementation:* 
 * At the end of the Busreg form, generate a document (operational report with some details filled and stored in attachments linked to the form) 
or use the contact generated at the final step, that will be digital signed.
Consideration: Create the signature as a reusable subflow 

*Example*

!image-2026-02-16-00-37-24-460.png|width=685,height=402!

*Documentation*
Document all the above adjustments. 

 

*Non functional requirements*
It is expected team to get aligned with respective teams and reassure that is not creating issues or the related NFRs will be tested :
Performance , Security, Accessibility, Usability 
DODs should be fulfilled.

+Security+
Certificates and private keys must be stored securely (e.g., HSM, secure vault, encrypted storage) or other repository. 
Access to signing functionality must be restricted and auditable.

+Auditability+
Every signing action must be logged:
Who/what triggered the signing
Timestamp
Document ID
Certificate used

+Performance+
Signing should not block critical user flows beyond acceptable SLA limits.
Support async signing for large documents or batch processing.

+Configurability+
Be able to select different configurations for digital signs  to be used.

Feature | IRM-30828 | CORE REVENUE MANAGEMENT CAPABILITIES | EXEMPTIONS | Introduce Exemptions | GRC | PI30 | 1213.1 | p3 | To Do | As a revenue authority I need to be able to implement Policy-driven exclusions for assessments and other liabilities ti the taxpayers to promote sectors, fairness, or development goals. (Other examples on their purposes :  Encourage social or economic development. , support specific sectors or vulnerable groups. , simplify tax administration for low-value cases. align with policy objectives (e.g., promoting investment, education, or sustainability) ) .

The exceptions may be of several *types* e.g. 
*Geographic* exemptions : to develop special zones
*Activity* exemptions : develop verticals based on Taxpayer activities exemptions  
*Party type* exemptions , *Party size* exemptions

*Introduction*

Already applied in system 
*Waivers:* Relief based on a discretionary decision to "forgive" or "cancel" a debt (mostly interest or penalty) 
It is applied after liability is assessed but before payment.
Amount is no longer collectible

{*}Write-offs{*}: An accounting action to remove an uncollectible debt from active accounts (not the same as forgiveness).
It is applied after the debt is confirmed and collectible. 
Amount is legally due but no longer pursued. 

*Suppression:* 
A temporary hold or administrative decision to suppress or defer issuing an assessment , interest.
It is applied during the assessment/process. 
The due amount exists but it is not communicated or enforced yet.  

New :
*Exemption:* 
A lawful exclusion from a tax obligation defined in legislation or policy.
It is applied before a due amount/liability arises. 
(e.g. Charitable organizations are exempt from income tax.)
The tax {*}never becomes due{*}—it’s not assessed or recorded as payable.

[Revenue type Registration]->  Apply Exemptions
[Obligations] ->  Exempt items excluded
Other: 
[Assessment]->  Suppressions may be applied
[Billing & Payment] ->   Waivers may be issued
[Collection/ Enforcement]->  Write-offs recorded
[Audit & Compliance]-> for all
 

*Functional Requirements*

*Admin :*
I can define Exception types [ Type, Status,  Period or permanent ,  Can be applied manually?,  Approvers list or profiles,  filters on how to define related audience/scope, filters on what will be exemptions requested, define details on the policy applied , legal reason/decision ]

I can apply Exceptions to taxpayers massively.  [Workflow,  Approvals,  Keep attachments, Keep contacts  , RTR and Obligations status , StartDate, EndDate, Status, Reason , timestamp, batch id ] 
 * Define approvers lists or profiles
 * Define approval process
 * Functionality on permanent or time defined exceptions
 * Define Legal bases
 * How to define scope
 * How to define targeted actions
 * Validations should be applied.

*User :*
I can apply Exceptions to taxpayers manually.  

*Addiitonally,*  
 * New statuses for Obligations
 * Balances review
 * Forms updated filters with exceptions
 * Traceability 
 * I can report on the exemptions applied

Feature | IRM-4293 | NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | EXTENSIBILITY | Define User-Defined Characteristics for Payment Event - Admin | Other | PI29 |  | p3 | Waiting Analysis Approval | As an admin, I want to define and maintain user-defined characteristics for payment events, so that these characteristics can be used to store data on instances of payment events.

*Functional Requirements*
 * Admin can define user-defined characteristics that must be available for a payment event
 * Admin can edit the properties of a user-defined characteristics, such as a unique identifier, description, help text, data type, data length, predefined value, lookup values, required, visible, and display only. Examples of data types that can be supported for these characteristics are string, date/time, number, amount, code list (e.g. region) and a reference to another type of entity in the application.
 * Reference Type of Entity
 ** Admin can define multiple user-defined characteristics that reference the same type of entity if instances of that type of entity can have a different meaning for a payment event
 ** Admin can define whether a user-defined characteristic can reference only one or multiple instances of a specific type of entity
 ** Admin can define what properties are shown for each type of entity that is referenced by a certain user-defined characteristic
 * Reference Code List
 ** Admin can define multiple user-defined characteristics that reference the same code list
 ** Admin can define whether a user-defined characteristic can reference only one or multiple code list items of a specific code list
 * Admin can remove a user-defined characteristic for a payment event if there are no referential constraints
 * Admin can disable a user-defined characteristic for a payment event if the characteristic is no longer relevant
 * Admin can enable a disabled user-defined characteristic for a payment event if the characteristic is deemed relevant again
 * Admin should be warned when adding or editing user-defined characteristics when payment events exist
 * Grouping
 ** Admin can group characteristics. Group can contain sub-groups.
 ** Admin can edit a group, for example the description
 ** Admin can delete a group, provided there are no referential constraints
 ** User can rearrange groups and sub-groups
 ** User can rearrange the characteristics within the payment event, groups or sub-groups
 * Rules
 ** Admin can define rules for a characteristic to validate the data that will be entered by the user
 ** Admin can define rules for a characteristic to determine if the characteristic should be visible or invisible
 ** Admin can define rules for a characteristic to determine if a characteristic is required or not
 ** Admin can define rules for a characteristic to determine when the characteristic should be editable or not
 ** Admin can define an error message that must be shown when the data entered by the user does not comply with the validation rule

Feature | IRM-30561 | NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | MAINTAINABILITY | After POC - Config Items Management ( Packaging & versioning) : Enable delivery teams to safely and selectively migrate configurations across environments /WIP | GRC | PI28 | 1280 | p3 | To Do | *AFTER POC*  [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-29268] 

{color:#ff8b00}*WIP  - Will be defined after POC* {color}
----
As a Solon Tax Delivery team, I need to be able to: 
-  safely and selectively, via guided steps, to migrate configurations across environments (Dev → Stg → Prod),
-  maintain versions of the configurations/other artifacts migrated to other environments and of the release/migration  (e.g. artifact version, release version)   
-  provide report on the results of the deployment process, 
-  see the history of the migrations, 
-  support zero/near-zero downtime deployments   (?)
-  support scheduled activation/ make effective the changes to destination environment,
-  enable team to flag changes as "ready to be migrated" , and capture ownership details
-  filter in a longer list of items based on predefine flags or versions the items to be added in the package for the migration,
-  enable team to select,  implementations, supporting them with  prechecks (Pre‑checks: environment compatibility, dependency resolution, conflict detection, schema compatibility, dry‑run simulation), dependencies and conflicts checks, 
-  provide rollback and recovery options,
-  enable team to select source and destination environments, 
-  ensure security, performance,  and compliance,
-  enforce governance with roles, performance and approval flows.

 

*Background:*
 
Configuration Data
 * Entity types (c_ objects) , Codelists/codelist items, , System parameters (codelist item attributes), 
queries, other config data (users, exchange rates, calendars, worker profiles, roles, object access groups, user access groups, ledgers, GL accounts numbers, rates etc), UI schemas/forms.'

Translations
 * Labels ( _l objects) 

TBC: 
 * (?) User defined characteristics,
 * Drools
 * (?) Other customizations

Ownerships 
 * Config items are flagged with its ownership , i.e. :  on who is responsible for their maintenance (Product team, national delivery team, or client-specific team) restricting areas that should not be used,  their intended scope of usage / applicability (global, regional, or specific clients) , whether they are reusable across implementations Additionally provide controlling mechanism on which items based on owner are eligible to be migrated (e.g. do not deploy base items, unless it is an attribute of a system parameter, entity schema help url, or labels.)   [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-26335]  

*Functional Requirements:*

*+Preparation+* 
 * *Prerequisites*
 ** Define environments that can be source and destinations
 ** Define the versioning numbering that will be used for all the items (?)
 * *Flag configuration items*
 ** Beforehand, the developer/admin should label Ownership of the component. 
 ** Beforehand, the developer/admin may label configurations implemented as  "Ready for export".  ([https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/PSD-11032)|https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/PSD-11032])
 ** Beforehand, version of the items to be migrated may be defined. 
 ** Beforehand, the developer/admin optionally may label the component with the Functionality or Scope or Product component will support.  
 ** Beforehand, the developer/admin may select if the Cong items will be activated while migrated or will remain inactive till admin manually activate them the destination environment. 
 ** Beforehand, the developer/admin may upload the file where applicable (labels - translations) should be uploaded. 
 ** Beforehand, the developer/admin may select the source and destination environments.  

 * *Roles and permissions*
 ** Permitted users can use the packaging tool and perform the mentioned actions

              consideration :  ? Could it be extended to use approval processes?

 

*+Core+*
 * *Ui*
 ** Admin may see the details of previous local releases/ deployments as well as historical data on the local releases/ deployments
 ** Admin/developer may check out and then check in any non Base config item
 *** Checked in item receives automatically a version
 *** Validation when trying to check out a Base item
 ** Admin may initiate a new deployment (create release) 
 *** Select source and destination environment
 *** UI or CLI to *select/export/inspect/import* configurations, code, flows, templates, etc.
 *** Select to proceed with the deployment
 *** Admin may use filters  (as per flags added above , version number ,  along with other items e.g. category field) to locate the items to be included in the package. 
 *** Admin can add comments per item and per local release. 
 ** Admin may see details under each logged release
 *** Admin can see timestamp and historical details on the local release. 
 *** Admin can see list of exceptions before and after the deployment
 ** Admin after deployment will be able to make effective/enable the version/selected items in destination environment. 

 

+*Deployment process*+

 
 * *Suggest items to be selected*
 ** Provide Delta support to select elements that are new or modified -  where applicable.
 ** Exclude BASE items with exceptions (help urls, labels, attributes in system parameters).
 ** Indicate possible conflicts.
 * *Dependency management*  - Select items to be migrated (metadata, content ... ) from a list .
 ** Identify dependencies and indicate what related items need to move together.
Identify and warn if related components must be exported together.
 ** Support  when certain settings (like endpoint URLs, external credentials, currency precision) may need to differ by environment - need a way to parameterize or externalize environment-specific config.)

 * *Standard Format & Packaging*
 ** Define a standard export/import format   (e.g., JSON, XML, YAML or other per component type) 
 ** Group exported artifacts into packages. 
 ** Be able to define the expiration date / inactivation date of an older version per component and have available mechanisms to validate that the new version will be available when old is expired. 
 *  *Import & Validation* : 
 ** Examine if needs to define states for each deployable (e.g., {_}Draft → Approved → Deployed → Deprecated{_}).
 ** Ensure compatibility and prevent unintended overwrites.
 ** Run automated validations in a dry run mode
 ** Indicate possible conflicts.
 ** Simulate a deployment before actual promotion
 ** Advice smoke testing after deployment

 * *Auditability and Reporting* 
 ** Audit Trail of  who changed what, when, and where in the target environment. (See also relevant section on  [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-27058] ) 
 ** Be able to see the result of the migration process. Monitor what succeeded, failed, or was skipped.
 
 * *Rollback Mechanism  / go back to a previous version*  
 ** Ability to revert a deployment if needed either fully or selectively.  See also relevant section on  [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-27058] 
 ** Ability to set when old version should be expired as new version should be active.  See also relevant section on  [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-27058] 

 * Compliance/ *Data security* privacy (Certain configuration or integration artifacts may handle sensitive data)
 ** Dev and Stg environments are created without taxpayer data, but include configuration and custom logic. i.e.,  when exporting from production to other envs, do not deploy data. 
 * Other
 ** Consider also translation management needs as described in  IRM-24809  

 

 

*Documentation*
 * Documentation will be delivered with the steps to install the application and tools needed plus how to use the tool with example. 

*Non Functional Requirements:*
 * Tool can be handled by delivery teams.
 * Performance and security DODs should be considered.

Feature | IRM-30679 | NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | MAINTAINABILITY | Vanilla Installation automation - Solon Tax kubernetes operator | Other | PI30 | 746.9 | p3 | To Do | *Problem Statement*

The current installation procedure for SolonTax (until v2.1.0 ) relies on the manual configuration and deployment of multiple Helm charts for core and auxiliary components. This process presents several challenges:
 * *High Operational Overhead:* System administrators must manually configure multiple {{values.yaml}} files, which is time-consuming.
 * *Prone to Errors:* There is a significant risk of misconfiguration when values are not synchronized correctly across different Helm charts (e.g. service endpoints).
 * *Complex Upgrades:* Managing the upgrade sequence and dependencies between components is a manual and fragile process.

*Proposed Solution*

To address these challenges, this feature proposes the development of a new Kubernetes Operator, the {*}SolonTax Operator{*}. The operator will act as a single point of control to automate and streamline the lifecycle management (installation, configuration, and upgrades) of a SolonTax environment.

By defining a Custom Resource (CR), administrators will be able to declare the desired state of a SolonTax installation, and the operator will work to fulfill that state, abstracting away the complexity of managing the underlying Helm charts.

*Acceptance Criteria*
 # *Helm Chart Orchestration:* The operator utilizes the existing {{Revenue Management}} and {{ISS}} Helm charts to deploy SolonTax components.
 # *Selective Component Installation:* The operator's Custom Resource (CR) allows specifying the installation of:
 ** {{Revenue Management}} components only.
 ** {{ISS}} components only.
 ** Both {{Revenue Management}} and {{ISS}} components.
 # *Configuration Cascading:* A single, top-level configuration value in the operator's CR (e.g., {{{}spec.env.jdbcUrl{}}}) is correctly propagated to all relevant underlying Helm charts and their respective ConfigMaps.
 # *Configuration Overrides:* The operator's CR provides a mechanism to override specific values in individual Helm charts (e.g., setting {{spec.components.revenueManagement.deployment.apiGateway.logging.level.root }}to {{DEBUG}} should override the default log level for that component only).
 # *Dependency Management:* The operator's reconciliation loop correctly manages dependencies. For example, it must ensure a database migration Job completes successfully before proceeding with the upgrade of dependent microservice Deployments.

*Technical Requirements & Considerations*
 * *Technology Stack:* The operator must be implemented using the *Java Operator SDK* ([https://github.com/operator-framework/java-operator-sdk]) and the *Spring Boot Starter* ([https://github.com/operator-framework/josdk-spring-boot-starter]).
 * *Helm Chart Dependency Strategy:* An architectural decision must be made on how the operator will access the Helm charts it manages. The implementation should consider and evaluate:
 ** Bundling the Helm charts within the operator's container image.
 ** Fetching the charts from a remote Helm registry at runtime.
 ** A hybrid approach that supports both.

*Out of Scope*
 * The initial version of this operator will *only* manage the core *SolonTax* components ({{{}Revenue Management{}}} and {{{}ISS{}}}).
 * The management of auxiliary components (e.g., databases, message brokers, logging stacks) is not included in the scope of this work but may be considered for future iterations.

Feature | IRM-37867 | NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | MAINTAINABILITY | Allowed Unicode characters to be used in 'Code' fields of configuration records (Excl.: Registration/Taxpayer Accounting) | GRC | PI28 | 448 | p1 | Ready for Dev | As an admin I need to be able to use several unicode characters in code fields that can be technically allowed to be used as to explain in code in localized text the short configuration name. 

 

*Functional Requirements* 

(BE & UI)
 * Defined Whitelist for "Code" fields of configuration entity types : 
*A)* A–Z, a–z, 0–9  
*B)* - (dash), _ (underscore),. (dot)
*C)*  Unicode characters for multilingual/localized alphabets,  e.g. ,  Greek , Swedish, Lithuanian, Spanish, Italian, French, Chinese.... 
 * Apply the validation to all Solon Tax Config entity types. If invalid characters are added validations will be thrown.

Document all the above adjustments. 

*Non functional requirements*

Performance , Security, Accessibility, Usability

----
Notes: 
 - Some config types are completed because of the linked bugs
 - By Sec team : Since Unicode will be supported, the validation has to be done after normalization of Unicode characters. Otherwise, special characters could still be accepted. For example ‘\u003C’ will be converted to the less than sign ‘<’.
 - The  “ “space , “:” (colon) will not be included because they may produce issues with data exports/migrations  and formatting. Other characters were excluded/avoided because of their usage in systems and difficulties that may produce while not be necessary, or because of security considerations.
 - Assumption : Records with Unicode Code characters are visible in UI properly, and  are searchable
Feature | IRM-32746 | NON-FUNCTIONAL REQUIREMENT COVERAGE | TRACEABILITY | Audit Log - Ability to keep Audit trail for authorization /LEFTOVER | GRC | PI28 | 739.2 | p2 | Waiting Analysis Approval | Leftover from [https://jira.intrasoft-intl.com/browse/IRM-29504] 

In some situations (no parent child relationship) , the audit log entries don’t include the information needed to display them in a single, unified list under the parent item or under each related entity.
Example: 
In practice, this means that a codelist can have multiple versions, and each codelist item can also have multiple versions. However, the audit log records for a codelist item are not grouped under one codelist version (or live record). Instead, they are distributed across the various versions, depending on when (version of codelist)  each event was logged.

This affects the following: 

*authorization-management MS*
    c_object_access_group_included_entity
    c_role_securable_object
